    "we thank amir mohammadi for many useful discussions relating to all aspects of this project . in particular some of the ideas for the proof of theorem  [",
    "theorem : main : partone ] came during discussions with amir mohammadi .",
    "we also thank vadim kaimanovich and emmanuel breuillard for their insights into the work of benoist and quint and elon lindenstrauss for his helpful comments .",
    "the theorems of  [ sec : theorems ] are inspired by the results of several authors on unipotent flows on homogeneous spaces , and in particular by ratner s seminal work .",
    "in particular , the analogues of theorem  [ theorem : p : measures ] and theorem  [ theorem : closure : submanifold ] in homogeneous dynamics are due to ratner @xcite , @xcite , @xcite , @xcite .",
    "( for an introduction to these ideas , and also to the proof by margulis and tomanov @xcite see the book @xcite . )",
    "the homogeneous analogue of the fact that @xmath48-invariant measures are @xmath0-invariant is due to mozes @xcite and is based on ratner s work .",
    "all of these results are based in part on the `` polynomial divergence '' of the unipotent flow on homogeneous spaces .",
    "however , in our setting , the dynamics of the unipotent flow ( i.e. the action of @xmath44 ) on @xmath23 is poorly understood , and plays no role in our proofs . the main strategy is to replace the `` polynomial divergence '' of unipotents by the `` exponential drift '' idea in the recent breakthrough paper by benoist and quint @xcite .",
    "one major difficulty is that we have no apriori control over the lyapunov spectrum of the geodesic flow ( i.e. the action of @xmath45 ) .",
    "by @xcite the lyapunov spectrum is simple for the case of lebesgue ( i.e. masur - veech ) measure , but for the case of an arbitrary @xmath48-invariant measure this is not always true , see e.g. @xcite , @xcite .    in order to use the the benoist - quint exponential drift argument , we must show that the zariski closure ( or more precisely the algebraic hull , as defined by zimmer @xcite ) of the kontsevich - zorich cocycle is semisimple .",
    "the proof proceeds in the following steps :    * step 1 .",

    "this difficulty is easily handled by working instead with the linear maps @xmath2870 and @xmath2871 .",
    "the second difficulty is connected to the first .",

    "the contents of this section are well - known , see e.g. @xcite , @xcite and also @xcite .",
    "however , for technical reasons , the statements we need do not formally follow from the results of any of the above papers .",
    "our setting is intermediate between the homogeneous dynamics setting of @xcite and the general @xmath4470-diffeomorphism on a compact manifold setup of @xcite , but it is closer to the former than the latter .",
    "what follows is a lightly edited but almost verbatim reproduction of @xcite , adapted to the setting of teichmller space .",
    "it is included here primarily for the convenience of the reader .",
    "the ( minor ) differences between our presentation and that of @xcite are related to the lack of uniform hyperbolicity outside of compact subsets of the space , and some notational changes due to the fact that our space is not homogeneous .",

  "abstract_text": [
    "<S> we prove some ergodic - theoretic rigidity properties of the action of @xmath0 on moduli space . </S>",
    "<S> in particular , we show that any ergodic measure invariant under the action of the upper triangular subgroup of @xmath0 is supported on an invariant affine submanifold .    </S>",
    "<S> the main theorems are inspired by the results of several authors on unipotent flows on homogeneous spaces , and in particular by ratner s seminal work . </S>"
